# Introduction | Hyperliquid

A TypeScript SDK for the [Hyperliquid API](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api)
.

npm

pnpm

yarn

bun

deno

Copy

    npm i @nktkas/hyperliquid

Copy

    pnpm add @nktkas/hyperliquid

Copy

    yarn add @nktkas/hyperliquid

Copy

    bun add @nktkas/hyperliquid

Copy

    deno add jsr:@nktkas/hyperliquid

**Type Safe**

100% TypeScript. Full inference for 80+ methods.

**Tested**

Types validated against real API responses.

**Minimal**

Few dependencies. Tree-shakeable.

**Universal**

Node.js, Deno, Bun, browsers, React Native.

**Transports**

Native [fetch](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Fetch_API)
 and [WebSocket](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/WebSocket)
.

**Wallet Support**

Works with [viem](https://viem.sh/)
 and [ethers](https://ethers.org/)
.

**Open Source**

MIT licensed on [GitHub](https://github.com/nktkas/hyperliquid)
.

* * *

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid#examples)

Examples


----------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid#read-data)

Read Data

Copy

    import { HttpTransport, InfoClient } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const client = new InfoClient({ transport: new HttpTransport() });
    
    // Order book
    const book = await client.l2Book({ coin: "ETH" });
    //    ^? { coin: string, time: number, levels: [{ px: string, sz: string, n: number }[], ...] }
    
    // Account state
    const state = await client.clearinghouseState({ user: "0x..." });
    //    ^? { marginSummary: {...}, assetPositions: [...], withdrawable: string }

Every method has fully typed parameters and responses. No more guessing what the API returns.

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid#place-orders)

Place Orders

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid#real-time-updates)

Real-time Updates

[NextInstallation](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/getting-started/installation)

Last updated 8 days ago

*   [Examples](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid#examples)
    
*   [Read Data](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid#read-data)
    
*   [Place Orders](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid#place-orders)
    
*   [Real-time Updates](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid#real-time-updates)
    

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport: new HttpTransport(),
      wallet: privateKeyToAccount("0x..."),
    });
    
    const result = await client.order({
      orders: [{\
        a: 4, // Asset index (ETH)\
        b: true, // Buy side\
        p: "3000", // Price\
        s: "0.1", // Size\
        r: false, // Reduce only\
        t: { limit: { tif: "Gtc" } },\
      }],
      grouping: "na",
    });
    // ^? { status: "ok", response: { type: "order", data: { statuses: [...] } } }

Copy

    import { SubscriptionClient, WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const client = new SubscriptionClient({ transport: new WebSocketTransport() });
    
    await client.l2Book({ coin: "ETH" }, (book) => {
      console.log(book.coin, book.levels[0][0].px);
      //          ^? { coin: string, time: number, levels: [...] }
    });

# Installation | Hyperliquid

Install the SDK via your package manager or a `<script>` tag.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/getting-started/installation#package-manager)

Package Manager


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

npm

pnpm

yarn

bun

deno

Copy

    npm i @nktkas/hyperliquid

Copy

    pnpm add @nktkas/hyperliquid

Copy

    yarn add @nktkas/hyperliquid

Copy

    bun add @nktkas/hyperliquid

Copy

    deno add jsr:@nktkas/hyperliquid

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/getting-started/installation#cdn)

CDN


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------

If you're not using a package manager, you can use the SDK via an ESM-compatible CDN such as [esm.sh](https://esm.sh/)
. Simply add a `<script type="module">` tag to the bottom of your HTML file with the following content:

Copy

    <script type="module">
      import * as hl from "https://esm.sh/jsr/@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    </script>

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/getting-started/installation#platform-requirements)

Platform Requirements


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Node.js Requires **Node.js 20** or higher.

Node.js 22+ includes native WebSocket support. For earlier versions, install the `ws` package if you plan to use `WebSocketTransport`:

Copy

    npm install ws

Copy

    import WebSocket from "ws";
    import * as hl from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new hl.WebSocketTransport({
      reconnect: {
        WebSocket, // Pass WebSocket class from ws package
      },
    });

React Native React Native requires polyfills for `TextEncoder` and `EventTarget`. Install and import them before the SDK:

[PreviousIntroduction](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid)
[NextQuick Start](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/getting-started/quick-start)

Last updated 8 days ago

*   [Package Manager](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/getting-started/installation#package-manager)
    
*   [CDN](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/getting-started/installation#cdn)
    
*   [Platform Requirements](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/getting-started/installation#platform-requirements)
    

Copy

    npm install fast-text-encoding event-target-polyfill

Copy

    import "fast-text-encoding";
    import "event-target-polyfill";
    import * as hl from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";

# Transports | Hyperliquid

A Transport is the layer responsible for executing requests to Hyperliquid servers.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#httptransport)

HttpTransport


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Executes requests via HTTP POST to the Hyperliquid API.

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#import)

Import

Copy

    import { HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#usage)

Usage

Copy

    import { HttpTransport, InfoClient } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const client = new InfoClient({ transport });
    
    const mids = await client.allMids();

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#parameters)

Parameters

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#istestnet-optional)

isTestnet (optional)

*   **Type:** `boolean`
    
*   **Default:** `false`
    

Use testnet endpoints instead of mainnet.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#timeout-optional)

timeout (optional)

*   **Type:** `number` | `null`
    
*   **Default:** `10000`
    

Request timeout in milliseconds. Set to `null` to disable.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#apiurl-optional)

apiUrl (optional)

*   **Type:** `string` | `URL`
    
*   **Default:** `https://api.hyperliquid.xyz` (mainnet) or `https://api.hyperliquid-testnet.xyz` (testnet)
    

Custom API URL for info and exchange requests.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#rpcurl-optional)

rpcUrl (optional)

*   **Type:** `string` | `URL`
    
*   **Default:** `https://rpc.hyperliquid.xyz` (mainnet) or `https://rpc.hyperliquid-testnet.xyz` (testnet)
    

Custom RPC URL for explorer requests (block details, transactions).

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#fetchoptions-optional)

fetchOptions (optional)

*   **Type:** [`RequestInit`](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/RequestInit)
    

Custom options passed to the underlying [`fetch`](https://developer.mozilla.org/en-US/docs/Web/API/Fetch_API)
 call.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#websockettransport)

WebSocketTransport


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

WebSocket connection for [subscriptions](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/websocket/subscriptions)
 and [POST requests](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/websocket/post-requests)
.

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#import-1)

Import

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#usage-1)

Usage

Subscription:

POST request:

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#reconnection)

Reconnection

When connection drops, the transport automatically reconnects with exponential backoff (max 10 seconds) and 3 attempts.

After reconnection, all active subscriptions are automatically restored if `resubscribe: true` (default).

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#parameters-1)

Parameters

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#istestnet-optional-1)

isTestnet (optional)

*   **Type:** `boolean`
    
*   **Default:** `false`
    

Use testnet endpoints instead of mainnet.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#timeout-optional-1)

timeout (optional)

*   **Type:** `number` | `null`
    
*   **Default:** `10000`
    

Request timeout in milliseconds. Set to `null` to disable.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#url-optional)

url (optional)

*   **Type:** `string` | `URL`
    
*   **Default:** `wss://api.hyperliquid.xyz/ws` (mainnet) or `wss://api.hyperliquid-testnet.xyz/ws` (testnet)
    

Custom WebSocket URL.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#reconnect-optional)

reconnect (optional)

*   **Type:** `object`
    
*   **Default:** `{ maxRetries: 3, connectionTimeout: 10000, reconnectionDelay: (attempt) => Math.min(~~(1 << attempt) * 150, 10000) }`
    

Reconnection policy. See [`ReconnectingWebSocketOptions`](https://github.com/nktkas/rews#options)
.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#resubscribe-optional)

resubscribe (optional)

*   **Type:** `boolean`
    
*   **Default:** `true`
    

Automatically restore active subscriptions after reconnection.

[PreviousQuick Start](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/getting-started/quick-start)
[NextClients](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients)

Last updated 8 days ago

*   [HttpTransport](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#httptransport)
    
*   [Import](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#import)
    
*   [Usage](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#usage)
    
*   [Parameters](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#parameters)
    
*   [WebSocketTransport](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#websockettransport)
    
*   [Import](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#import-1)
    
*   [Usage](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#usage-1)
    
*   [Reconnection](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#reconnection)
    
*   [Parameters](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#parameters-1)
    

Copy

    const transport = new HttpTransport({
      isTestnet: true,
    });

Copy

    const transport = new HttpTransport({
      timeout: 30000,
    });

Copy

    const transport = new HttpTransport({
      apiUrl: "https://custom-api.example.com",
    });

Copy

    const transport = new HttpTransport({
      rpcUrl: "https://custom-rpc.example.com",
    });

Copy

    const transport = new HttpTransport({
      fetchOptions: {
        headers: {
          "X-Custom-Header": "value",
        },
      },
    });

Copy

    import { WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";

Copy

    import { SubscriptionClient, WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport();
    const client = new SubscriptionClient({ transport });
    
    const subscription = await client.allMids((data) => {
      console.log(data.mids);
    });

Copy

    import { InfoClient, WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport();
    const client = new InfoClient({ transport });
    
    const mids = await client.allMids();

Copy

    const transport = new WebSocketTransport({
      isTestnet: true,
    });

Copy

    const transport = new WebSocketTransport({
      timeout: 30000,
    });

Copy

    const transport = new WebSocketTransport({
      url: "wss://custom-api.example.com/ws",
    });

Copy

    const transport = new WebSocketTransport({
      reconnect: {
        maxRetries: 10,
        reconnectionDelay: 1000, // fixed 1s delay
      },
    });

Copy

    const transport = new WebSocketTransport({
      resubscribe: false, // handle resubscription manually
    });

---

# Quick Start | Hyperliquid

Get started with the SDK in just a few lines of code.

1

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/getting-started/quick-start#set-up-transport)

Set up Transport

First, create a [Transport](https://github.com/nktkas/hyperliquid/blob/main/core-concepts/transports/README.md)
 — the layer that handles communication with Hyperliquid servers.

HttpTransport

WebSocketTransport

Use [`HttpTransport`](https://github.com/nktkas/hyperliquid/blob/main/core-concepts/transports/README.md#httptransport)
 for simple requests.

Copy

    import { HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();

Use [`WebSocketTransport`](https://github.com/nktkas/hyperliquid/blob/main/core-concepts/transports/README.md#websockettransport)
 for subscriptions or lower latency.

Copy

    import { WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport();

2

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/getting-started/quick-start#create-a-client)

Create a Client

Next, create a [Client](https://github.com/nktkas/hyperliquid/blob/main/core-concepts/clients/README.md)
 with your transport. The SDK provides three clients for different purposes:

InfoClient

ExchangeClient

SubscriptionClient

Use [`InfoClient`](https://github.com/nktkas/hyperliquid/blob/main/core-concepts/clients/README.md#infoclient)
 to query market data, account state, and other read-only information.

Copy

    import { HttpTransport, InfoClient } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    
    const client = new InfoClient({ transport });
    
    // Get mid prices for all assets
    const mids = await client.allMids();
    // => { "BTC": "97000.5", "ETH": "3500.25", ... }

Use [`ExchangeClient`](https://github.com/nktkas/hyperliquid/blob/main/core-concepts/clients/README.md#exchangeclient)
 to place orders, transfer funds, and perform other actions that require signing.

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    
    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport,
      wallet: privateKeyToAccount("0x..."), // viem account or ethers signer
    });
    
    // Place a limit order
    const result = await client.order({
      orders: [{\
        a: 0, // Asset index (0 = BTC)\
        b: true, // Buy side\
        p: "95000", // Price\
        s: "0.01", // Size\
        r: false, // Not reduce-only\
        t: { limit: { tif: "Gtc" } },\
      }],
      grouping: "na",
    });
    // => { status: "ok", response: { type: "order", data: { statuses: [...] } } }

Use [`SubscriptionClient`](https://github.com/nktkas/hyperliquid/blob/main/core-concepts/clients/README.md#subscriptionclient)
 to subscribe to live market data via WebSocket.

[PreviousInstallation](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/getting-started/installation)
[NextTransports](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports)

Last updated 8 days ago

Copy

    import { SubscriptionClient, WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport();
    
    const client = new SubscriptionClient({ transport });
    
    // Subscribe to all mid prices
    const subscription = await client.allMids((data) => {
      console.log("Price update:", data.mids);
    });
    
    // Later: unsubscribe
    await subscription.unsubscribe();

---

# Error Handling | Hyperliquid

All SDK errors extend `HyperliquidError`, making it easy to catch SDK-specific errors.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#error-hierarchy)

Error Hierarchy


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    HyperliquidError
    ├── TransportError
    │   ├── HttpRequestError
    │   └── WebSocketRequestError
    ├── ApiRequestError
    └── AbstractWalletError

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#hyperliquiderror)

HyperliquidError


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Base class for all SDK errors.

Copy

    import { HyperliquidError } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    try {
      await client.order({ ... });
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof HyperliquidError) {
        // Any SDK error
      }
    }

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#transporterror)

TransportError


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Thrown when an error occurs at the transport level (network issues, timeouts).

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#httprequesterror)

HttpRequestError

Thrown when an HTTP request fails.

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#websocketrequesterror)

WebSocketRequestError

Thrown when a WebSocket request fails.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#apirequesterror)

ApiRequestError


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Thrown when the Hyperliquid API returns an error response. Contains the full response for inspection.

Common API errors:

*   `"User or API Wallet 0x... does not exist"` — invalid signer or signature
    
*   `"Insufficient margin to place order"` — not enough balance
    
*   `"Price too far from oracle"` — price outside allowed range
    

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#abstractwalleterror)

AbstractWalletError


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Thrown when wallet operations fail (signing, getting address).

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#validation-errors)

Validation Errors


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Request parameters are validated before sending. Invalid parameters throw [`ValiError`](https://valibot.dev/api/ValiError/)
 from [valibot](https://valibot.dev/)
.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#example-comprehensive-error-handling)

Example: Comprehensive Error Handling


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[PreviousClients](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients)
[NextInfo Methods](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/api-reference/info-methods)

Last updated 8 days ago

*   [Error Hierarchy](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#error-hierarchy)
    
*   [HyperliquidError](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#hyperliquiderror)
    
*   [TransportError](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#transporterror)
    
*   [HttpRequestError](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#httprequesterror)
    
*   [WebSocketRequestError](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#websocketrequesterror)
    
*   [ApiRequestError](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#apirequesterror)
    
*   [AbstractWalletError](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#abstractwalleterror)
    
*   [Validation Errors](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#validation-errors)
    
*   [Example: Comprehensive Error Handling](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling#example-comprehensive-error-handling)
    

Copy

    import { HttpRequestError } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    try {
      await client.allMids();
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof HttpRequestError) {
        console.log(error.response); // Response object
        console.log(error.body); // Response body text
      }
    }

Copy

    import { WebSocketRequestError } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    try {
      await client.allMids();
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof WebSocketRequestError) {
        console.log(error.message);
      }
    }

Copy

    import { ApiRequestError } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    try {
      await client.order({ ... });
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof ApiRequestError) {
        console.log(error.message);  // Extracted error message
        console.log(error.response); // Full API response
      }
    }

Copy

    import { AbstractWalletError } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    try {
      await client.order({ ... });
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof AbstractWalletError) {
        console.log(error.message);
      }
    }

Copy

    import * as v from "valibot";
    
    try {
      await client.order({
        orders: [{\
          a: -1, // invalid: must be non-negative\
          // ...\
        }],
        grouping: "na",
      });
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof v.ValiError) {
        console.log(error.issues); // Validation issues
      }
    }

Copy

    import {
      AbstractWalletError,
      ApiRequestError,
      HttpRequestError,
      HyperliquidError,
      WebSocketRequestError,
    } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import * as v from "valibot";
    
    try {
      const result = await client.order({ ... });
    } catch (error) {
      if (error instanceof v.ValiError) {
        // Invalid parameters (before request)
        console.error("Validation failed:", error.issues);
      } else if (error instanceof ApiRequestError) {
        // API returned an error
        console.error("API error:", error.message);
      } else if (error instanceof HttpRequestError) {
        // HTTP request failed
        console.error("HTTP error:", error.response?.status);
      } else if (error instanceof WebSocketRequestError) {
        // WebSocket request failed
        console.error("WebSocket error:", error.message);
      } else if (error instanceof AbstractWalletError) {
        // Wallet operation failed
        console.error("Wallet error:", error.message);
      } else if (error instanceof HyperliquidError) {
        // Other SDK error
        console.error("SDK error:", error.message);
      } else {
        // Unknown error
        throw error;
      }
    }

---

# Clients | Hyperliquid

Clients provide methods to interact with the Hyperliquid API. Each client corresponds to a specific API type.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#infoclient)

InfoClient


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Read-only access to market data, user state, and other public information. Corresponds to the [Info endpoint](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/info-endpoint)
.

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#import)

Import

Copy

    import { InfoClient } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#usage)

Usage

Copy

    import { HttpTransport, InfoClient } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const client = new InfoClient({ transport });
    
    // Get all mid prices
    const mids = await client.allMids();
    
    // Get user's perpetual positions
    const state = await client.clearinghouseState({
      user: "0x...",
    });

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#parameters)

Parameters

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#transport-required)

transport (required)

*   **Type:** [`HttpTransport`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#httptransport)
     | [`WebSocketTransport`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#websockettransport)
    

The transport used to send requests.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#exchangeclient)

ExchangeClient


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Execute actions: place orders, cancel orders, transfer funds, etc. Corresponds to the [Exchange endpoint](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/exchange-endpoint)
.

Requires a wallet for signing. The SDK handles [signing](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/signing)
 and [nonces](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/nonces-and-api-wallets)
 automatically.

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#import-1)

Import

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#usage-with-viem)

Usage with viem

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#usage-with-ethers)

Usage with ethers

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#usage-with-multi-sig)

Usage with Multi-Sig

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#parameters-1)

Parameters

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#transport-required-1)

transport (required)

*   **Type:** [`HttpTransport`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#httptransport)
     | [`WebSocketTransport`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#websockettransport)
    

The transport used to send requests.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#wallet-required-for-single-wallet)

wallet (required for single wallet)

*   **Type:** `AbstractWallet`
    

The wallet used to sign requests. Supports:

*   **viem:** [Local accounts](https://viem.sh/docs/accounts/local)
    , [JSON-RPC accounts](https://viem.sh/docs/accounts/jsonRpc)
    
*   **ethers:** [Wallet](https://docs.ethers.org/v6/api/wallet/)
    , [JsonRpcSigner](https://docs.ethers.org/v6/api/providers/jsonrpc/#JsonRpcSigner)
    
*   Any object with `address` and `signTypedData` method
    

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#signers-required-for-multi-sig)

signers (required for multi-sig)

*   **Type:** `[AbstractWallet, ...AbstractWallet[]]`
    

Array of wallets for multi-sig signing. The first wallet is the [leader](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/hypercore/multi-sig)
.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#multisiguser-required-for-multi-sig)

multiSigUser (required for multi-sig)

*   **Type:** `` `0x${string}` ``
    

The multi-signature account address.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#signaturechainid-optional)

signatureChainId (optional)

*   **Type:** `` `0x${string}` `` | `(() => MaybePromise<`0x${string}`>)`
    
*   **Default:** Wallet's connected chain ID
    

Custom chain ID for EIP-712 signing.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#defaultvaultaddress-optional)

defaultVaultAddress (optional)

*   **Type:** `` `0x${string}` ``
    

Default vault address for vault-based operations. Can be overridden per-request.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#defaultexpiresafter-optional)

defaultExpiresAfter (optional)

*   **Type:** `number` | `(() => MaybePromise<number>)`
    

Default expiration time in milliseconds for actions. See [Expires After](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/exchange-endpoint#expires-after)
.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#noncemanager-optional)

nonceManager (optional)

*   **Type:** `(address: string) => MaybePromise<number>`
    
*   **Default:** Timestamp-based with auto-increment
    

Custom nonce generator. See [Hyperliquid nonces](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/nonces-and-api-wallets#hyperliquid-nonces)
.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#subscriptionclient)

SubscriptionClient


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Real-time data via WebSocket subscriptions. Corresponds to [WebSocket subscriptions](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/websocket/subscriptions)
.

**Requires** [`**WebSocketTransport**`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#websockettransport)
**.**

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#import-2)

Import

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#usage-1)

Usage

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#subscription-object)

Subscription Object

Each subscription returns an object with:

*   `unsubscribe()` — Stop receiving updates
    
*   `failureSignal` — AbortSignal that aborts if resubscription fails after reconnect
    

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#parameters-2)

Parameters

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#transport-required-2)

transport (required)

*   **Type:** [`WebSocketTransport`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#websockettransport)
    

Must be [`WebSocketTransport`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#websockettransport)
. Does not work with [`HttpTransport`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#httptransport)
.

[PreviousTransports](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports)
[NextError Handling](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/error-handling)

Last updated 7 days ago

*   [InfoClient](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#infoclient)
    
*   [Import](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#import)
    
*   [Usage](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#usage)
    
*   [Parameters](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#parameters)

*   [Usage with ethers](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#usage-with-ethers)

Copy

    const client = new InfoClient({
      transport: new HttpTransport(),
    });

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const wallet = privateKeyToAccount("0x...");
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    
    const client = new ExchangeClient({ transport, wallet });
    
    // Place a limit order
    const result = await client.order({
      orders: [{\
        a: 0, // asset index (BTC)\
        b: true, // buy\
        p: "50000", // price\
        s: "0.01", // size\
        r: false, // not reduce-only\
        t: { limit: { tif: "Gtc" } },\
      }],
      grouping: "na",
    });

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { ethers } from "ethers";
    
    const wallet = new ethers.Wallet("0x...");
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    
    const client = new ExchangeClient({ transport, wallet });

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const signer1 = privateKeyToAccount("0x...");
    const signer2 = privateKeyToAccount("0x...");
    
    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport: new HttpTransport(),
      signers: [signer1, signer2], // any number of signers
      multiSigUser: "0x...", // multi-sig account address
    });

Copy

    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport,
      wallet,
      signatureChainId: "0xa4b1", // Arbitrum One
    });

Copy

    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport,
      wallet,
      defaultVaultAddress: "0x...",
    });
    
    // Uses defaultVaultAddress
    await client.order({ ... });
    
    // Override for this request
    await client.order({ ... }, { vaultAddress: "0x..." });

Copy

    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport,
      wallet,
      defaultExpiresAfter: 60000, // 1 minute
    });

Copy

    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport,
      wallet,
      nonceManager: async (address) => Date.now(),
    });

Copy

    import { SubscriptionClient } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";

Copy

    import { SubscriptionClient, WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport();
    const client = new SubscriptionClient({ transport });
    
    // Subscribe to all mid prices
    const subscription = await client.allMids((data) => {
      console.log(data.mids);
    });
    
    // Later: unsubscribe
    await subscription.unsubscribe();

Copy

    const subscription = await client.trades({ coin: "BTC" }, (data) => {
      console.log(data);
    });
    
    subscription.failureSignal.addEventListener("abort", (event) => {
      console.error("Subscription failed:", event.target.reason);
    });

Copy

    const client = new SubscriptionClient({
      transport: new WebSocketTransport(),
    });

      "response": {
        "type": "order",
        "data": {
          "statuses": [\
            {\
              "resting": {\
                "oid": 1,\
                "cloid": "text"\
              }\
            }\
          ]
        }
      }
    }

# Symbol Converter | Hyperliquid

Utility for converting human-readable asset symbols to Hyperliquid asset IDs.

Hyperliquid uses numeric asset IDs internally:

*   **Perpetuals:** `0`, `1`, `2`, ... (index in `meta.universe`)
    
*   **Spot:** `10000 + index` (e.g., `10107` for HYPE/USDC)
    
*   **Builder DEX:** `100000 + dex_index * 10000 + asset_index`
    

See [Asset IDs](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/asset-ids)
 in Hyperliquid docs.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter#import)

Import


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    import { SymbolConverter } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils";

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter#usage)

Usage


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    import { HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { SymbolConverter } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const converter = await SymbolConverter.create({ transport });
    
    // Perpetual
    converter.getAssetId("BTC"); // 0
    converter.getSzDecimals("BTC"); // 5
    
    // Spot market (BASE/QUOTE format)
    converter.getAssetId("HYPE/USDC"); // 10107
    converter.getSzDecimals("HYPE/USDC"); // 2
    converter.getSpotPairId("HYPE/USDC"); // "@107"

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter#with-builder-dex)

With Builder DEX


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Builder DEX assets require explicit opt-in:

Copy

    // Load specific dexs
    const converter = await SymbolConverter.create({
      transport,
      dexs: ["test"], // load only "test" dex
    });
    
    // Or load all dexs
    const converter = await SymbolConverter.create({
      transport,
      dexs: true, // load all available dexs
    });
    
    converter.getAssetId("test:ABC"); // 110000

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter#methods)

Methods


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter#getassetid)

getAssetId

Returns the numeric asset ID for use in exchange requests.

Copy

    converter.getAssetId("BTC"); // 0 (perpetual)
    converter.getAssetId("HYPE/USDC"); // 10107 (spot)
    converter.getAssetId("test:ABC"); // 110000 (builder dex)
    converter.getAssetId("UNKNOWN"); // undefined

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter#getszdecimals)

getSzDecimals

Returns the size decimals for an asset. Used for formatting order sizes and prices.

Copy

    converter.getSzDecimals("BTC"); // 5 → size like "0.00001"
    converter.getSzDecimals("HYPE/USDC"); // 2 → size like "0.01"

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter#getspotpairid)

getSpotPairId

Returns the spot pair ID for info endpoints and subscriptions (l2Book, trades, etc.).

Copy

    converter.getSpotPairId("HYPE/USDC"); // "@107"
    converter.getSpotPairId("PURR/USDC"); // "PURR/USDC" (special case)

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter#reload)

reload

Refreshes asset mappings from the API. Useful when new assets are listed.

Copy

    await converter.reload();

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter#parameters)

Parameters


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter#transport-required)

transport (required)

*   **Type:** [`HttpTransport`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#httptransport)
     | [`WebSocketTransport`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/transports#websockettransport)
    

Transport instance for API requests.

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter#dexs-optional)

dexs (optional)

*   **Type:** `string[]` | `boolean`
    
*   **Default:** `false`
    

Builder DEX support:

*   `false` or omitted — don't load builder dexs
    
*   `true` — load all available dexs
    
*   `["dex1", "dex2"]` — load only specified dexs
    

Copy

    // Don't load dexs (default)
    await SymbolConverter.create({ transport });
    
    // Load all dexs
    await SymbolConverter.create({ transport, dexs: true });
    
    // Load specific dexs
    await SymbolConverter.create({ transport, dexs: ["test"] });

[PreviouswebData3](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/api-reference/subscription-methods/webdata3)
[NextFormatting](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting)

Last updated 8 days ago

---

# Formatting | Hyperliquid

Utilities for formatting prices and sizes according to Hyperliquid's [tick and lot size rules](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/tick-and-lot-size)
.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting#import)

Import


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    import { formatPrice, formatSize } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils";

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting#formatprice)

formatPrice


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Formats a price according to Hyperliquid rules:

*   Maximum 5 significant figures
    
*   Maximum `(6 - szDecimals)` decimal places for perps, `(8 - szDecimals)` for spot
    
*   Integer prices are always allowed regardless of significant figures
    

Copy

    import { formatPrice } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils";
    
    // Perpetual (default)
    formatPrice("1234.5", 0); // "1234.5" ✓
    formatPrice("1234.56", 0); // "1234.5" (truncated to 5 sig figs)
    formatPrice("0.001234", 0); // "0.001234" ✓
    formatPrice("0.0012345", 0); // "0.001234" (truncated to 5 sig figs)
    
    // Spot market
    formatPrice("0.0001234", 0, "spot"); // "0.0001234" ✓
    formatPrice("0.00012345", 2, "spot"); // "0.000123" (max 6 decimals for szDecimals=2)
    
    // Integer prices always allowed
    formatPrice("123456", 0); // "123456" ✓

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting#parameters)

Parameters

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting#price-required)

price (required)

*   **Type:** `string` | `number`
    

The price to format.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting#szdecimals-required)

szDecimals (required)

*   **Type:** `number`
    

Size decimals of the asset. Get from [`SymbolConverter.getSzDecimals()`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter#getszdecimals)
 or `meta` response.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting#type-optional)

type (optional)

*   **Type:** `"perp"` | `"spot"`
    
*   **Default:** `"perp"`
    

Market type. Affects maximum decimal places (6 for perp, 8 for spot).

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting#throws)

Throws

*   `RangeError` — if the formatted price becomes `0` after truncation
    

Copy

    formatPrice("0.0000001", 0); // throws RangeError: Price is too small and was truncated to 0

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting#formatsize)

formatSize


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Formats a size by truncating to `szDecimals` decimal places.

Copy

    import { formatSize } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils";
    
    formatSize("1.23456789", 5); // "1.23456"
    formatSize("1.23456789", 2); // "1.23"
    formatSize("1.999", 0); // "1"

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting#parameters-1)

Parameters

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting#size-required)

size (required)

*   **Type:** `string` | `number`
    

The size to format.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting#szdecimals-required-1)

szDecimals (required)

*   **Type:** `number`
    

Size decimals of the asset. Get from [`SymbolConverter.getSzDecimals()`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter#getszdecimals)
 or `meta` response.

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting#throws-1)

Throws

*   `RangeError` — if the formatted size becomes `0` after truncation (prevents accidentally closing entire position)
    

Copy

    formatSize("0.001", 2); // throws RangeError: Size is too small and was truncated to 0

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting#example-placing-an-order)

Example: Placing an Order


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { formatPrice, formatSize, SymbolConverter } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/utils";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const converter = await SymbolConverter.create({ transport });
    const client = new ExchangeClient({ transport, wallet });
    
    const symbol = "BTC";
    const assetId = converter.getAssetId(symbol); // 0
    const szDecimals = converter.getSzDecimals(symbol); // 5
    
    const price = formatPrice("97123.456789", szDecimals); // "97123"
    const size = formatSize("0.00123456789", szDecimals); // "0.00123"
    
    await client.order({
      orders: [{\
        a: assetId,\
        b: true,\
        p: price,\
        s: size,\
        r: false,\
        t: { limit: { tif: "Gtc" } },\
      }],
      grouping: "na",
    });

[PreviousSymbol Converter](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/symbol-converter)
[NextSigning](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing)

Last updated 8 days ago

---

# Signing | Hyperliquid

Low-level utilities for signing Hyperliquid transactions. Most users don't need this — [`ExchangeClient`](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/core-concepts/clients#exchangeclient)
 handles signing automatically.

Use these utilities when:

*   **Custom wallet integration** — implement `AbstractViemLocalAccount` to use hardware wallets, MPC, or other signing systems
    
*   **Signing unsupported actions** — sign new action types that are not yet implemented in the SDK
    

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#import)

Import


------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    import {
      createL1ActionHash,
      PrivateKeySigner,
      signL1Action,
      signMultiSigAction,
      signUserSignedAction,
    } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#privatekeysigner)

PrivateKeySigner


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Lightweight signer that doesn't require viem or ethers.

Copy

    import { PrivateKeySigner } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";
    
    const signer = new PrivateKeySigner("0xabc123...");
    console.log(signer.address); // "0x..."

Use with `ExchangeClient`:

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { PrivateKeySigner } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";
    
    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport: new HttpTransport(),
      wallet: new PrivateKeySigner("0x..."),
    });

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#signl1action)

signL1Action


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Signs an L1 action — trading operations like orders, cancels, leverage updates, TWAP, vault operations, etc.

Copy

    import { signL1Action } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const wallet = privateKeyToAccount("0x...");
    
    const action = {
      type: "cancel",
      cancels: [{ a: 0, o: 12345 }],
    };
    const nonce = Date.now();
    
    const signature = await signL1Action({ wallet, action, nonce });
    
    // Send manually
    const response = await fetch("https://api.hyperliquid.xyz/exchange", {
      method: "POST",
      headers: { "Content-Type": "application/json" },
      body: JSON.stringify({ action, signature, nonce }),
    });

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#parameters)

Parameters

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#wallet-required)

wallet (required)

*   **Type:** `AbstractWallet`
    

Wallet to sign (viem, ethers, or PrivateKeySigner).

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#action-required)

action (required)

*   **Type:** `Record<string, unknown>`
    

Action object. Key order matters for hash calculation.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#nonce-required)

nonce (required)

*   **Type:** `number`
    

Timestamp in milliseconds.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#istestnet-optional)

isTestnet (optional)

*   **Type:** `boolean`
    
*   **Default:** `false`
    

Use testnet instead of mainnet.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#vaultaddress-optional)

vaultAddress (optional)

*   **Type:** `` `0x${string}` ``
    

[Vault address](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/exchange-endpoint#subaccounts-and-vaults)
 for trading on behalf of a vault.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#expiresafter-optional)

expiresAfter (optional)

*   **Type:** `number`
    

[Expiration time](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/exchange-endpoint#expires-after)
 of the action in milliseconds since epoch.

The action hash depends on key order. Use valibot schema to guarantee correct order:

Copy

    import { CancelByCloidRequest } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange";
    import * as v from "valibot";
    
    const action = v.parse(CancelByCloidRequest.entries.action, {
      cancels: [{ cloid: 12345, asset: 0 }],
      type: "cancel",
    });
    // => { type, cancels: [{ asset, cloid }] }

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#signusersignedaction)

signUserSignedAction


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Signs a user-signed action — transfers and administrative operations like withdraw, usdSend, spotSend, approveAgent, etc. Uses EIP-712 typed data with `signatureChainId`.

Copy

    import { signUserSignedAction } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";
    import { ApproveAgentTypes } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const wallet = privateKeyToAccount("0x...");
    
    const action = {
      type: "approveAgent",
      signatureChainId: "0x66eee",
      hyperliquidChain: "Mainnet",
      agentAddress: "0x...",
      agentName: "MyAgent",
      nonce: Date.now(),
    };
    
    const signature = await signUserSignedAction({
      wallet,
      action,
      types: ApproveAgentTypes,
    });

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#parameters-1)

Parameters

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#wallet-required-1)

wallet (required)

*   **Type:** `AbstractWallet`
    

Wallet to sign (viem, ethers, or PrivateKeySigner).

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#action-required-1)

action (required)

*   **Type:** `object`
    

Action object with `signatureChainId` field.

#### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#types-required)

types (required)

*   **Type:** `object`
    

EIP-712 types for the action. Import from `@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange` (e.g., `ApproveAgentTypes`).

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#signmultisigaction)

signMultiSigAction


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Signs a multi-signature action. Requires signatures from multiple signers collected beforehand.

Copy

    import { signL1Action, signMultiSigAction } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const multiSigUser = "0x..."; // multi-sig account address
    const signerKeys = ["0x...", "0x..."]; // private keys of all signers
    const leader = privateKeyToAccount(signerKeys[0] as `0x${string}`);
    
    const action = {
      type: "scheduleCancel",
      time: Date.now() + 10000,
    };
    const nonce = Date.now();
    
    // Collect signatures from all signers
    const signatures = await Promise.all(
      signerKeys.map((key) =>
        signL1Action({
          wallet: privateKeyToAccount(key as `0x${string}`),
          action: [multiSigUser.toLowerCase(), leader.address.toLowerCase(), action],
          nonce,
          isTestnet: false,
        })
      ),
    );
    
    // Sign the multi-sig wrapper
    const multiSigAction = {
      type: "multiSig",
      signatureChainId: "0x66eee",
      signatures,
      payload: {
        multiSigUser,
        outerSigner: leader.address,
        action,
      },
    };
    
    const signature = await signMultiSigAction({
      wallet: leader,
      action: multiSigAction,
      nonce,
    });

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#createl1actionhash)

createL1ActionHash


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Creates a hash of an L1 action without signing. Used internally by `signL1Action` as `connectionId` in EIP-712 structure. The hash depends on key order in the action object.

Copy

    import { createL1ActionHash } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";
    
    const action = {
      type: "cancel",
      cancels: [{ a: 0, o: 12345 }],
    };
    
    const hash = createL1ActionHash({
      action,
      nonce: Date.now(),
    });
    // => "0x..."

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing#abstractwallet)

AbstractWallet


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

The SDK accepts any wallet that implements `signTypedData`. Supported out of the box:

*   **viem:** [Local accounts](https://viem.sh/docs/accounts/local)
    , [JSON-RPC accounts](https://viem.sh/docs/accounts/jsonRpc)
    
*   **ethers:** [Wallet](https://docs.ethers.org/v6/api/wallet/)
    , [JsonRpcSigner](https://docs.ethers.org/v6/api/providers/jsonrpc/#JsonRpcSigner)
    
*   Any object with `address` and `signTypedData` method
    

Copy

    // viem
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    const wallet = privateKeyToAccount("0x...");
    
    // ethers
    import { Wallet } from "ethers";
    const wallet = new Wallet("0x...");
    
    // SDK (no viem or ethers dependency)
    import { PrivateKeySigner } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/signing";
    const wallet = new PrivateKeySigner("0x...");

[PreviousFormatting](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/formatting)
[NextTree-shaking](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking)

# Tree-shaking | Hyperliquid

The SDK supports tree-shaking through granular imports — reduce bundle size by ~50% by importing only the functions you need.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#import)

Import


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    // Granular imports (tree-shakeable)
    import { clearinghouseState } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/info";
    import { order } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange";
    import { candle } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/subscription";

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#usage)

Usage


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------

Functions have the same names as client methods. Instead of `client.order(...)`, you call `order(config, ...)`:

Copy

    import { HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { order } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    const wallet = privateKeyToAccount("0x...");
    
    // Function takes config as first argument
    const result = await order(
      { transport, wallet },
      {
        orders: [{\
          a: 0,\
          b: true,\
          p: "30000",\
          s: "0.1",\
          r: false,\
          t: { limit: { tif: "Gtc" } },\
        }],
        grouping: "na",
      },
    );

Compare with client approach:

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#info-functions)

Info Functions


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Info functions only need `transport`:

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#subscription-functions)

Subscription Functions


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Subscription functions require `WebSocketTransport`:

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#available-exports)

Available Exports


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Export Path

Description

`@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/info`

Info API functions (`clearinghouseState`, `meta`, `allMids`, etc.)

`@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange`

Exchange API functions (`order`, `cancel`, `withdraw3`, etc.)

`@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/subscription`

Subscription functions (`candle`, `trades`, `l2Book`, etc.)

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#valibot-schemas)

Valibot Schemas


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

These exports also include [valibot](https://valibot.dev/)
 schemas for every API method:

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#available-schemas)

Available Schemas

Each method exports:

*   `*Request` — full request schema (with `type`, `nonce`, `signature` for exchange)
    
*   `*Response` — response schema from API
    

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#use-cases)

Use Cases

**TypeScript types:**

**Runtime validation:**

**Field descriptions:**

Schemas include descriptions for all fields via `v.description()`, useful for generating documentation or exploring the API structure.

[PreviousSigning](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/utilities/signing)
[NextCLI](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli)

Last updated 8 days ago

*   [Import](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#import)
    
*   [Usage](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#usage)
    
*   [Info Functions](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#info-functions)
    
*   [Subscription Functions](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#subscription-functions)
    
*   [Available Exports](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#available-exports)
    
*   [Valibot Schemas](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#valibot-schemas)
    
*   [Available Schemas](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#available-schemas)
    
*   [Use Cases](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/tree-shaking#use-cases)
    

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport: new HttpTransport(),
      wallet: privateKeyToAccount("0x..."),
    });
    
    // Method on client instance
    const result = await client.order({
      orders: [{\
        a: 0,\
        b: true,\
        p: "30000",\
        s: "0.1",\
        r: false,\
        t: { limit: { tif: "Gtc" } },\
      }],
      grouping: "na",
    });

Copy

    import { HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { allMids } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/info";
    
    const transport = new HttpTransport();
    
    const mids = await allMids({ transport });

Copy

    import { WebSocketTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { trades } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/subscription";
    
    const transport = new WebSocketTransport();
    
    const subscription = await trades({ transport }, { coin: "BTC" }, (data) => {
      console.log(data);
    });

Copy

    import { ClearinghouseStateRequest, ClearinghouseStateResponse } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/info";
    import { OrderRequest, OrderResponse } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange";

Copy

    import { ClearinghouseStateResponse } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/info";
    import * as v from "valibot";
    
    type State = v.InferOutput<typeof ClearinghouseStateResponse>;

Copy

    import { OrderRequest } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid/api/exchange";
    import * as v from "valibot";
    
    // Validate data before sending
    const validated = v.parse(OrderRequest, {
      action: {
        type: "order",
        orders: [{ a: 0, b: true, p: "30000", s: "0.1", r: false, t: { limit: { tif: "Gtc" } } }],
        grouping: "na",
      },
      nonce: Date.now(),
      signature: { r: "0x...", s: "0x...", v: 27 },
    });

# CLI | Hyperliquid

Command-line interface for interacting with Hyperliquid API without writing code.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli#usage)

Usage


--------------------------------------------------------------------

Copy

    npx @nktkas/hyperliquid <endpoint> <method> [options]

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli#endpoint)

endpoint

*   **Type:** `"info"` | `"exchange"`
    

API endpoint to use:

*   `info` — query market data and account state
    
*   `exchange` — execute trading operations (requires `--private-key`)
    

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli#method)

method

Method name matching the SDK client methods (e.g., `allMids`, `order`, `cancel`).

Run `npx @nktkas/hyperliquid --help` for the full list.

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli#testnet)

\--testnet

Use testnet instead of mainnet.

Copy

    npx @nktkas/hyperliquid info allMids --testnet

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli#timeout)

\--timeout

*   **Type:** `number`
    
*   **Default:** `10000`
    

Request timeout in milliseconds.

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli#private-key)

\--private-key

*   **Type:** `` `0x${string}` ``
    

Private key for exchange operations. Required for `exchange` endpoint.

> \[!WARNING\] Passing private keys via command line is insecure. Use environment variables:

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli#vault)

\--vault

*   **Type:** `` `0x${string}` ``
    

Vault address for trading on behalf of a vault.

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli#offline)

\--offline

Generate request payload without sending. Useful for debugging or signing transactions offline.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli#examples)

Examples


--------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli#info-endpoint)

Info Endpoint

### 

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli#exchange-endpoint)

Exchange Endpoint

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli#json-arguments)

JSON Arguments


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Some methods require JSON arguments. Escape quotes properly for your shell:

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli#output)

Output


----------------------------------------------------------------------

CLI outputs JSON to stdout. Format with [jq](https://jqlang.org/)
 or PowerShell:

    # Get all mid prices
    npx @nktkas/hyperliquid info allMids

    npx @nktkas/hyperliquid info portfolio --user 0x...

      --orders '[{"a":0,"b":true,"p":"30000","s":"0.1","r":false,"t":{"limit":{"tif":"Gtc"}}}]'

      --cancels '[{"a":0,"o":12345}]'

      --destination 0x... --amount 100.5

    npx @nktkas/hyperliquid info allMids | ConvertFrom-Json | ConvertTo-Json -Depth 10

# FAQ | Hyperliquid

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/faq#how-to-create-a-market-order)

How to create a market order?


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Hyperliquid doesn't have traditional market orders. Use a limit order with `tif: "Ioc"` (Immediate or Cancel) and a price that guarantees immediate execution:

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport, InfoClient } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const info = new InfoClient({ transport: new HttpTransport() });
    const exchange = new ExchangeClient({
      transport: new HttpTransport(),
      wallet: privateKeyToAccount("0x..."),
    });
    
    // Get current price
    const mids = await info.allMids();
    const currentPrice = parseFloat(mids["ETH"]);
    
    // Buy: set price above current (e.g., +1%)
    const buyPrice = currentPrice * 1.01;
    
    // Sell: set price below current (e.g., -1%)
    const sellPrice = currentPrice * 0.99;
    
    await exchange.order({
      orders: [{\
        a: 4,\
        b: true,\
        p: buyPrice,\
        s: "0.1",\
        r: false,\
        t: { limit: { tif: "Ioc" } }, // Immediate or Cancel\
      }],
      grouping: "na",
    });

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/faq#how-to-use-agent-wallet)

How to use Agent Wallet?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[Agent wallets](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/nonces-and-api-wallets#api-wallets)
 can sign on behalf of your master account. Use the agent's private key instead of master account's:

Create an agent via `approveAgent` method or through the [Hyperliquid UI](https://app.hyperliquid.xyz/API)
.

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/faq#how-to-trade-on-behalf-of-a-vault-or-sub-account)

How to trade on behalf of a Vault or Sub-Account?


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Pass [vault or sub-account address](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/exchange-endpoint#subaccounts-and-vaults)
 via `vaultAddress` option:

[](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/faq#how-to-sign-with-metamask-or-other-browser-wallets)

How to sign with MetaMask or other browser wallets?


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

L1 actions use chain ID `1337` (dev network, not in wallets by default) and sign an action hash instead of readable order details. Users will see `Agent { source: "a", connectionId: "0x..." }` — not useful.

**Solution:** Use [Agent Wallet](https://hyperliquid.gitbook.io/hyperliquid-docs/for-developers/api/nonces-and-api-wallets#api-wallets)
 for trading. Master account signs once to approve the agent.

[PreviousCLI](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/cli)

Last updated 7 days ago

*   [How to create a market order?](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/faq#how-to-create-a-market-order)
    
*   [How to use Agent Wallet?](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/faq#how-to-use-agent-wallet)
    
*   [How to trade on behalf of a Vault or Sub-Account?](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/faq#how-to-trade-on-behalf-of-a-vault-or-sub-account)
    
*   [How to sign with MetaMask or other browser wallets?](https://nktkas.gitbook.io/hyperliquid/other/faq#how-to-sign-with-metamask-or-other-browser-wallets)
    

Copy

    import { ExchangeClient, HttpTransport } from "@nktkas/hyperliquid";
    import { privateKeyToAccount } from "viem/accounts";
    
    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport: new HttpTransport(),
      wallet: privateKeyToAccount("0x..."), // agent's private key
    });

Copy

    // Per-request
    await client.order({ ... }, { vaultAddress: "0x..." });
    
    // Or set default for all requests
    const client = new ExchangeClient({
      transport: new HttpTransport(),
      wallet: privateKeyToAccount("0x..."),
      defaultVaultAddress: "0x...",
    });

---
